{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_013YGNAPbUAuoT2BeJ6qUy6M","type":"tool_result","content":"{\"content\":\"1: # Code Coverage Summary\\n2: \\n3: <div align=\\\"center\\\">\\n4: \\n5: ![.NET 6.0](https://img.shields.io/badge/Version-.NET%206.0-informational?style=flat&logo=dotnet)\\n6: &nbsp;\\n7: ![Built With Docker](https://img.shields.io/badge/Built_With-Docker-informational?style=flat&logo=docker)\\n8: &nbsp;\\n9: [![OpenSSF Best Practices](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/6292/badge)](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/6292)\\n10: &nbsp;\\n11: [![CI Build](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/ci-build.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/ci-build.yml)\\n12: &nbsp;\\n13: [![CodeQL Scan](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/codeql-scan.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/codeql-scan.yml)\\n14: \\n15: </div>\\n16: \\n17: A GitHub Action that reads Cobertura format code coverage files from your test suite and outputs a text or markdown summary. This summary can be posted as a Pull Request comment or included in Release Notes by other actions to give you an immediate insight into the health of your code without using a third-party site.\\n18: \\n19: Code Coverage Summary is designed for use with any test framework that outputs coverage in Cobertura XML format including [Coverlet](https://github.com/coverlet-coverage/coverlet), [gcovr](https://github.com/gcovr/gcovr), [simplecov](https://github.com/simplecov-ruby/simplecov) and [MATLAB](https://uk.mathworks.com/help/matlab/ref/matlab.unittest.plugins.codecoverageplugin-class.html). See the [FAQ](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/wiki/Frequently-Asked-Questions#which-testing-tools-does-ccs-work-with) for more details. If it doesn't work with your tooling please [open an issue][new-issue] to discuss the problem.\\n20: \\n21: Code Coverage Summary is compatible with [StepSecurity Secure Workflows](https://github.com/step-security/secure-workflows) and uses a Docker image that is cryptographically signed using [Sigstore](https://www.sigstore.dev/). For instructions how to verify the Docker image please see the [Wiki](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/wiki/Verify-the-Docker-Image).\\n22: \\n23: **As a Docker based action Code Coverage Summary requires a Linux runner.**\\n24: \\n25: \\n26: ## Inputs\\n27: \\n28: ### `filename`\\n29: **Required**\\n30: \\n31: A comma separated list of code coverage files to analyse. Also supports using glob patterns to match multiple files. If there are any spaces in a path or filename this value must be in quotes.\\n32: \\n33: \\n34: ### `badge`\\n35: \\n36: Include a badge reporting the Line Rate coverage in the output using [shields.io](https://shields.io/) - `true` or `false` (default).\\n37: \\n38: Line Rate | Badge\\n39: --------- | -----\\n40: less than lower threshold (50%) | ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-45%25-critical?style=flat)\\n41: between thresholds (50% - 74%) | ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-65%25-yellow?style=flat)\\n42: equal or greater than upper threshold (75%) | ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-83%25-success?style=flat)\\n43: \\n44: See [`thresholds`](#thresholds) to change these values.\\n45: \\n46: \\n47: ### `fail_below_min`\\n48: \\n49: Fail the workflow if the overall Line Rate is below lower threshold - `true` or `false` (default). The default lower threshold is 50%, see [`thresholds`](#thresholds).\\n50: \\n51: \\n52: ### `format`\\n53: \\n54: Output Format - `markdown` or `text` (default).\\n55: \\n56: \\n57: ### `hide_branch_rate`\\n58: \\n59: Hide Branch Rate metrics in the output - `true` or `false` (default).\\n60: \\n61: \\n62: ### `hide_complexity`\\n63: \\n64: Hide Complexity metrics in the output - `true` or `false` (default).\\n65: \\n66: \\n67: ### `indicators`\\n68: \\n69: Include health indicators in the output - `true` (default) or `false`.\\n70: \\n71: Line Rate | Indicator\\n72: --------- | ---------\\n73: less than lower threshold (50%) | ❌\\n74: between thresholds (50% - 74%) | ➖\\n75: equal or greater than upper threshold (75%) | ✔\\n76: \\n77: See [`thresholds`](#thresholds) to change these values.\\n78: \\n79: \\n80: ### `output`\\n81: \\n82: Output Type - `console` (default), `file` or `both`.\\n83: \\n84: `console` will output the coverage summary to the GitHub Action log.\\n85: \\n86: `file` will output the coverage summary to `code-coverage-results.txt` for text or `code-coverage-results.md` for markdown format in the workflow's working directory.\\n87: \\n88: `both` will output the coverage summary to the Action log and a file as above.\\n89: \\n90: \\n91: ### `thresholds`\\n92: \\n93: Lower and upper threshold percentages for badge and health indicators, lower threshold can also be used to fail the action. Separate the values with a space and enclose them in quotes; default `'50 75'`.\\n94: \\n95: \\n96: ## Outputs\\n97: \\n98: ### Text Example\\n99: ```\\n100: https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-83%25-success?style=flat\\n101: \\n102: Company.Example: Line Rate = 83%, Branch Rate = 69%, Complexity = 671, ✔\\n103: Company.Example.Library: Line Rate = 27%, Branch Rate = 100%, Complexity = 11, ❌\\n104: Summary: Line Rate = 83% (1212 / 1460), Branch Rate = 69% (262 / 378), Complexity = 682, ✔\\n105: Minimum allowed line rate is 50%\\n106: ```\\n107: \\n108: \\n109: ### Markdown Example\\n110: \\n111: > ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-83%25-success?style=flat)\\n112: > \\n113: > Package | Line Rate | Branch Rate | Complexity | Health\\n114: > -------- | --------- | ----------- | ---------- | ------\\n115: > Company.Example | 83% | 69% | 671 | ✔\\n116: > Company.Example.Library | 27% | 100% | 11 | ❌\\n117: > **Summary** | **83%** (1212 / 1460) | **69%** (262 / 378) | 682 | ✔\\n118: > \\n119: > _Minimum allowed line rate is `50%`_\\n120: \\n121: \\n122: ## Usage\\n123: \\n124: ```yaml\\n125: name: Code Coverage Summary Report\\n126: uses: irongut/CodeCoverageSummary@v1.3.0\\n127: with:\\n128:   filename: coverage.cobertura.xml\\n129: ```\\n130: \\n131: \\n132: ### .Net Workflow Example\\n133: \\n134: ```yaml\\n135: name: .Net 6 CI Build\\n136: \\n137: on:\\n138:   push:\\n139:     branches: [ master ]\\n140:   pull_request:\\n141:     branches: [ master ]\\n142: \\n143: jobs:\\n144:   build:\\n145:     runs-on: ubuntu-latest\\n146:     name: CI Build\\n147:     steps:\\n148:     - name: Checkout\\n149:       uses: actions/checkout@v2\\n150: \\n151:     - name: Setup .NET\\n152:       uses: actions/setup-dotnet@v1\\n153:       with:\\n154:         dotnet-version: 6.0.x\\n155: \\n156:     - name: Restore Dependencies\\n157:       run: dotnet restore src/Example.sln\\n158: \\n159:     - name: Build\\n160:       run: dotnet build src/Example.sln --configuration Release --no-restore\\n161: \\n162:     - name: Test\\n163:       run: dotnet test src/Example.sln --configuration Release --no-build --verbosity normal --collect:\\\"XPlat Code Coverage\\\" --results-directory ./coverage\\n164: \\n165:     - name: Code Coverage Report\\n166:       uses: irongut/CodeCoverageSummary@v1.3.0\\n167:       with:\\n168:         filename: coverage/**/coverage.cobertura.xml\\n169:         badge: true\\n170:         fail_below_min: true\\n171:         format: markdown\\n172:         hide_branch_rate: false\\n173:         hide_complexity: true\\n174:         indicators: true\\n175:         output: both\\n176:         thresholds: '60 80'\\n177: \\n178:     - name: Add Coverage PR Comment\\n179:       uses: marocchino/sticky-pull-request-comment@v2\\n180:       if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'\\n181:       with:\\n182:         recreate: true\\n183:         path: code-coverage-results.md\\n184: ```\\n185: \\n186: \\n187: ## Version Numbers\\n188: \\n189: Version numbers will be assigned according to the [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/) scheme.\\n190: This means, given a version number MAJOR.MINOR.PATCH, we will increment the:\\n191: \\n192: 1. MAJOR version when we make incompatible API changes\\n193: 2. MINOR version when we add functionality in a backwards compatible manner\\n194: 3. PATCH version when we make backwards compatible bug fixes\\n195: \\n196: \\n197: ## Contributing\\n198: \\n199: ### Report Bugs\\n200: \\n201: Please make sure the bug is not already reported by searching existing [issues].\\n202: \\n203: If you're unable to find an existing issue addressing the problem please [open a new one][new-issue]. Be sure to include a title and clear description, as much relevant information as possible, a workflow sample and any logs demonstrating the problem.\\n204: \\n205: \\n206: ### Suggest an Enhancement\\n207: \\n208: Please [open a new issue][new-issue].\\n209: \\n210: \\n211: ### Submit a Pull Request\\n212: \\n213: Discuss your idea first, so that your changes have a good chance of being merged in.\\n214: \\n215: Submit your pull request against the `master` branch.\\n216: \\n217: Pull requests that include documentation and relevant updates to README.md are merged faster, because you won't have to wait for somebody else to complete your contribution.\\n218: \\n219: \\n220: ## License\\n221: \\n222: Code Coverage Summary is available under the MIT license, see the [LICENSE](LICENSE) file for more info.\\n223: \\n224: [issues]: https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/issues\\n225: [new-issue]: https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/issues/new\\n226: \",\"url\":\"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/CodeCoverageSummary--dibench@147e5d9d419019e95d6fa60e2373c4d785922c34/-/blob/README.md\"}"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a88e4850-dc3c-4e2b-ba9a-0c4495317be9","uuid":"e05c7d3f-ee52-4335-a78a-a30091b25a2a","tool_use_result":{"content":"{\"content\":\"1: # Code Coverage Summary\\n2: \\n3: <div align=\\\"center\\\">\\n4: \\n5: ![.NET 6.0](https://img.shields.io/badge/Version-.NET%206.0-informational?style=flat&logo=dotnet)\\n6: &nbsp;\\n7: ![Built With Docker](https://img.shields.io/badge/Built_With-Docker-informational?style=flat&logo=docker)\\n8: &nbsp;\\n9: [![OpenSSF Best Practices](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/6292/badge)](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/6292)\\n10: &nbsp;\\n11: [![CI Build](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/ci-build.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/ci-build.yml)\\n12: &nbsp;\\n13: [![CodeQL Scan](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/codeql-scan.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/actions/workflows/codeql-scan.yml)\\n14: \\n15: </div>\\n16: \\n17: A GitHub Action that reads Cobertura format code coverage files from your test suite and outputs a text or markdown summary. This summary can be posted as a Pull Request comment or included in Release Notes by other actions to give you an immediate insight into the health of your code without using a third-party site.\\n18: \\n19: Code Coverage Summary is designed for use with any test framework that outputs coverage in Cobertura XML format including [Coverlet](https://github.com/coverlet-coverage/coverlet), [gcovr](https://github.com/gcovr/gcovr), [simplecov](https://github.com/simplecov-ruby/simplecov) and [MATLAB](https://uk.mathworks.com/help/matlab/ref/matlab.unittest.plugins.codecoverageplugin-class.html). See the [FAQ](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/wiki/Frequently-Asked-Questions#which-testing-tools-does-ccs-work-with) for more details. If it doesn't work with your tooling please [open an issue][new-issue] to discuss the problem.\\n20: \\n21: Code Coverage Summary is compatible with [StepSecurity Secure Workflows](https://github.com/step-security/secure-workflows) and uses a Docker image that is cryptographically signed using [Sigstore](https://www.sigstore.dev/). For instructions how to verify the Docker image please see the [Wiki](https://github.com/irongut/CodeCoverageSummary/wiki/Verify-the-Docker-Image).\\n22: \\n23: **As a Docker based action Code Coverage Summary requires a Linux runner.**\\n24: \\n25: \\n26: ## Inputs\\n27: \\n28: ### `filename`\\n29: **Required**\\n30: \\n31: A comma separated list of code coverage files to analyse. Also supports using glob patterns to match multiple files. If there are any spaces in a path or filename this value must be in quotes.\\n32: \\n33: \\n34: ### `badge`\\n35: \\n36: Include a badge reporting the Line Rate coverage in the output using [shields.io](https://shields.io/) - `true` or `false` (default).\\n37: \\n38: Line Rate | Badge\\n39: --------- | -----\\n40: less than lower threshold (50%) | ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-45%25-critical?style=flat)\\n41: between thresholds (50% - 74%) | ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-65%25-yellow?style=flat)\\n42: equal or greater than upper threshold (75%) | ![Code Coverage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Code%20Coverage-83%25-success?style=flat)\\n43: \\n44: See [`thresholds`](#thresholds) to change these values.\\n45: \\n46: \\n47: ### `fail_below_min`\\n48: \\n49: Fail the workflow if the overall Line Rate is below lower threshold - `true` or `false` (default). The default lower threshold is 50%, see [`thresholds`](#thresholds).\\n50: \\n51: \\n52: ### `format`\\n53: \\n54: Output Format - `markdown` or `text` (default).\\n55: \\n56: \\n57: ### `hide_branch_rate`\\n58: \\n59: Hide Branch Rate metrics in the output - `true` or `false` (default).\\n60: \\n61: \\n62: ### `hide_complexity`\\n63: \\n64: Hide Complexity metrics in the output - `true` or `false` (default).\\n65: \\n66: \\n67: ### `indicators`\\n68: \\n69: Include health indicators in the output - `true` (default) or `false`.\\n70: \\n71: Line Rate | Indicator\\n72: --------- | ---------\\n73: less than lower threshold (50%) | ❌\\n74: between thresholds (50% - 74%) | ➖\\n75: equal or greater than upper threshold (75%) | ✔\\n76: \\n77: See [`thresholds`](#thresholds) to change these values.\\n78: \\n79: \\n80: ### `output`\\n81: \\n82: Output Type - `console` (default), `file` or `both`.\\n83: \\n84: `console` will output the coverage summary to the GitHub Action log.\\n85: \\n86: `file` will output the coverage summary to `code-coverage-results.txt` for text or `code-coverage-results.md` for markdown format in the workflow's working directory.\\n87: \\n88: `both` will output the coverage summary to the Action log and a file as above.\\n89: \\n90: \\n91: ### `thresholds`\\n92: \\n93: Lower and upper threshold percentages for badge and health indicators, lower threshold can also be used to fail the action.
